mso-break-type:section-break; page-break-before:always" /><div><h1 style="font-size:18pt; line-height:150%; margin:5pt 0pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:36.15pt"><a name="_Toc29462850"></a><a name="_Toc140422752"></a><a name="_Toc438923301"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">第一章</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">前言</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc29462850"></span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422752"></span></a></h1><h2 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc29462851"></a><a name="_Toc140422753"></a><a name="_Toc438923302"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">1.1  </span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">作业背景</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc29462851"></span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422753"></span></a></h2><div style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; clear:both; margin:0pt"><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">本文根据《</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">管理信息系统</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">》课程要求而做。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; padding-bottom:1pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image006.gif" width="38" height="38" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">课程作业要求如下：</span></p></div><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">用管理信息系统开发工具（例如</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Visual Basic</span><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Visual Foxpro</span><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Access</span><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">PowerBuilder</span><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Delphi</span><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">等）开发一个实用的中小型管理信息系统。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">1．根据课程设计时间选择适当规模大小的设计课题。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">2．根据合理的进度安排，按照系统开发的流程及方法，踏实地开展课程设计活动。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">3．课程设计过程中，根据选题的具体需求，在开发各环节中撰写相关的技术文档，最后提交详细的课程设计报告，</span><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">至少</span><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">包括系统可行性分析报告、系统分析报告、系统设计报告三个主要部分。</span></p><div style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; clear:both; margin:0pt"><p style="margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:华文楷体; font-size:12pt">4．开发出可以运行的管理信息系统，通过上机检查。</span></p><p style="margin:0pt; orphans:0; padding-bottom:1pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p></div><h2 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc29462852"></a><a name="_Toc140422754"></a><a name="_Toc438923303"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">1.2  </span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">选题说明</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc29462852"></span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422754"></span></a></h2><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">       </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">通过为润捷公司建设大农合电商平台，对农产品的生产经营情况有了比较清楚的了解</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对于公司目前所存在的问题也有了更好的认识。通过大量的调研访谈，为公司开发了生产管理系统</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">并撰写了此论文。</span></p><p style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; padding-bottom:1pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 19.5pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 19.5pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">(1)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">基本思路</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 19.5pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">运</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">用UML进行用例分析，运用java语言进行系统实现。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 19.5pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">(2)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">作业目标</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 19.5pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">进行业务分析</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">，</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">了解用户需求</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">，</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">最终</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">完成可以实际运行的管理信息系统。</span></p><p style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; padding-bottom:1pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><h2 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc29462853"></a><a name="_Toc140422755"></a><a name="_Toc438923304"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">1.3</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc29462853"></span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">  </span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">工作业绩</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422755"></span></a></h2><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">(1)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">小组</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">主要工作</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">完成</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">润杰公司的沛县大农合电子商务平台。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(2) </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">主要收获</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">要想了解到客户的真正需求，是需要通过大量的沟通。有的时候即使是客户自己说了自己的需求，但仍不是他真正想要的系统。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(3) </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">小组分工</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">黄家雯 订单，用户，供应商，采购，农户管理；邱丽：美工；陈景恒：网站前台；张鹏飞：部门，员工，权限，类别管理；</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(4) </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">自我评定    □优    □良   □中  □及格  □不及格</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">&#xa0;</span></p><br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both" /><p style="font-size:18pt; line-height:150%; margin:5pt 0pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:36.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422756"></a><a name="_Toc438923305"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">  </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">第</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">二</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">章</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422756"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">绪论</span></a></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422757"></a><a name="_Toc438923306"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">2</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">.1</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422757"></span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">公司简介</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">江苏润捷信息科技发展有限公司，注册资本</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3000</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">万，成立于</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2011</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">年</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">月</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">12</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">日，从事现代网络研究、农业物联网络研发、生产、销售、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">IT</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">解决方案、软件开发、信息推广应用与服务，是徐州唯一一家从事企业研究、生产及网络第三方服务型的科技型服务公司，且具有建筑智能化三级资质。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">位于江苏</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">徐州市泉山区集群路北侧徐州软件园</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">路</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">号徐州软件园</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">号研发办公楼</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">A</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">座。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司不断的跟踪国内外先进技术动态，加强新产品的研发工作，物联网技术的应用，利用现代电子技术、移动网络技术、计算机及网络技术相结合的技术。通过网络实时传输至远程中心服务器，中心服务器接收存储数据，结合对应的诊断知识模型对数据解析处理，以达到分布式监测，集中式管理。服务对象</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">依法为成员提供农业物联网、农业电子商务、农产品网络服务、电子科技、软件开发、以及与农业生产经营有关的技术、信息等服务</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">主要业务包括；</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">农产品的初加工、贮藏和销售。农产品的网上贸易代理及网上商务咨询。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">开展与农产品经营有关的技术信息咨询服务。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司本着</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">“</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">尊重、负责、诚信与法律遵从、和谐共生可持续发展</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">”</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的宗旨，积极拓宽服务范围，加强技能拓展，先后和东南大学、南京林业大学、南京农业大学、徐州工程学院等高等院企建立业务联系。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在这几年的艰苦创业中</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">润捷集团高举民族工业旗帜</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">以创民族品牌为己任</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">, </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">汲取中国文化之精髓</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">形成了独具特色的企业文化</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">无论是意蕴丰富的产品设计</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">, </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">严格有序的现代管理</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">卓有成效的人才培训</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">还是积极参与国际市场竞争</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">寻求</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">更广阔的合作空间</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">.</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">无不展示了润捷集团——</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">一个现代化民营企业的独特魅力。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">因此</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">我们有理由相信</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">凭借强大的实力、执着的信念、不懈的努力</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">越走越稳</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">越走越远</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">润捷</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的明天——无极限</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">! </span></p><p style="font-size:18pt; line-height:150%; margin:5pt 0pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:36.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422760"><br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both" /></a><a name="_Toc438923307"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">第三章</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">系统调查与问题分析</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422760"></span></a></p><h2 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422761"></a><a name="_Toc438923308"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">3.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">1</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422761"></span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">开发的背景</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">调查</span></a></h2><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923309"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.1.1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">企业现状调查</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">:</span></a><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">当下中国，电子商务正处在一个飞速发展的阶段，然而，我们又很容易的发现，电子商务在农业这一重要的领域还几乎是一片空白。我国农业目前问题颇多，一个很显著的问题就是菜价颇高，而消费者和菜农却都成了这其中的牺牲品。 如能精简流通环节，甚至是直接砍去中间环节，将有效解决相关问题。所以</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">润捷公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">为了适应市场</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">，</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">要取得突破性的发展</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">摆脱当前</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的各种不利因素</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">增强企业的竞争力</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">获得更大的企业效益。实行信息化管理的方式刻不容缓</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">只有增加企业管理的技术含量</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">缩减各种成本</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">才能在行业中站稳脚跟。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司目前的各种管理方式都是比较传统的</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">像销售</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">采购</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">生产</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">仓储</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">, </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">人事等各个环节的管理</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">企业都仍然是使用效率比较低</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">成本比较高的人工处理</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">方式。所以开发出一套能够及时处理信息和业务、反映问题的信息管理系统便十分必要和紧迫。这样既可以减少员工工作量</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">提高业务的实效性和准确性</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">又可以给管理层提供更准确更真实的资料以帮助其制定决策</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">而更为重要的是旨在适应集团市场化运作的大方针</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">保证走在其发展改革的前沿</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">赢得同行业的竞争。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923310"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.1.2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">企业存在的问题</span></a><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在客户、供应商、计划单管理、销售管理、订单管理、库存管理、</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">申请领料、审批领料、确认领料</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">人员管理</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">工资管理等操作上都是以原始的手</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">工单据来传递信息</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">带来的一系列问题就显而易见了</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">工作的冗余和繁琐</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">信息</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的不准确</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">管理的疏忽</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">材料的浪费</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">决策依据的不真实等大大影响了润捷</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的整体发展。而在供应商、销售客户的管理上现在企业还是一片空白</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">完全是依</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">据管理层多年企业管理的经验来进行决策。任何关于公司客户、供应商的信息都是难以掌握和察觉的</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">造成了市场开拓的困难和物质供应的不透明性。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">另外还有在实际管理中出现种种的漏洞</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">例如库存因为统计问题而造成流失</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">, </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">员工的工资因为一些中层领导的违规操作而背离实际情况</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">这些都会给企业带来</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">很大的损失。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所以这种落后的管理方式已经不能适应公司的长期发展</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">又尤其是在推进其市场化进程的阶段</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">面临着比较严峻的市场竞争的时候</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">企业更要团结一心</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">克</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">服各种阻力</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">开发一套基于公司现状的信息管理系统便被提上了议事日程。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923311"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.1.3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">系统开发的价值</span></a><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所谓管理信息系统是指一个由人和计算机等组成的</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">能进行信息收集、传输、</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">加工、保存、维护和使用的系统</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">而管理信息系统的最终目的是为决策者服务</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">, </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">提供适合企业发展的战略计划。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">管理的核心是决策</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">而管理信息系统可以辅助决策</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">特别是战略决策</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">它的好坏直接影响到企业的生存和发展。管理信息系统正在促使管理方法由定性向定性和定量相结合的方向发展</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">这表现在管理中运用了预测和各种数学模型来定量</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">分析企业中的问题并解决之。过去管理问题常常由于数据管理的不完善而难以进行</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">而管理信息系统则可以结合管理需要</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">提供充分的数据</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">为模拟和制定预测创造一定的环境。因此</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">润捷</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">需一套适合自己企业实际情况的管理信息系统</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对于企业的发展具有革命性的。便用计算机准确高效的处理方法和数据库紧凑严谨的结构</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">代替公司人员的手工操作和纸质传递</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">可以为企业创造更多的价值</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">可以增加企业的竞争力</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422762"></a><a name="_Toc438923312"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">3.2.</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422762"></span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">企业</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">管理职能问题分析</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt"><span style="display:none; font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; widows:0"><span style="color:#ff0000; font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><div style="text-align:center"><table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="border-collapse:collapse; margin:0 auto; width:530.35pt"><tr style="height:20.3pt"><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:96.5pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:13.3pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">部门</span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:193.55pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">职责</span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:207.15pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">问题</span></p></td></tr><tr style="height:90.45pt"><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:96.5pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">采购部 </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:193.55pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">负责公司面料</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">辅料的采购</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">；</span><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">负责原料的质量检测</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">；</span><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">3 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">根据订单的需求</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">有顺序的安排</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">采购计划</span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:207.15pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">由于订单较多</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">采购比较</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">混乱</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">；</span><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">由于辅料种类较多</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">容易</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">出现漏掉某种辅料采购。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span></p></td></tr><tr style="height:52.05pt"><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:96.5pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">销售部</span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:193.55pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">负责销售工作</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">维持客户关系</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">; </span><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">为客户解决产品方面的问题。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:207.15pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">办事效率低</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">客户的反馈</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">和投诉不能得到快捷有效的</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">处理</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">；</span><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">领导不能随时查看客户</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">反馈来的关于产品和市场的信息。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span></p></td></tr><tr style="height:31.55pt"><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:96.5pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">仓库管理 </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:193.55pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">原材料的保管</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">；</span><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">成品的保管</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:207.15pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">库存流失</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">；</span><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">具体存货不太清楚</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span></p></td></tr><tr style="height:27.55pt"><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:96.5pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">员工管理</span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:193.55pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">员工</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">工作分配；</span><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">上报</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">工作量</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:207.15pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:Times; font-size:9pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">效率低下</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt">经常无事可做。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:9pt"> </span></p></td></tr></table></div><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; widows:0"><span style="color:#ff0000; font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">表</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3-</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923313"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">3.3</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">针对</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">现状提出系统目</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">标</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">根据企业的实际业务流程设计系统的功能结构。系统必须能简化操作人员的工作量</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">使他们从繁琐的单据中摆脱出来</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">更多的关注如何提高管理的水平提高</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">管理的效益。系统能够为管理决策提供数据支持</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">保存信息</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">提供外界和内部各</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">方面的信息。同时</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在管理中能够为公司带来实实在在资源的节约。使企业在最短的时间内适应市场化的需求</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">立于竞争的不败之地。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司的管理效率不高</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">满足不了公司日益增加的业务需求</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">资源得不到有效的利用</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">与集团公司的市场化进程大相违背。因此</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">本系统从以下几个方面来满足公司的基本要求</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">: </span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923314"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.3.1</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">系统设计原则</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">:</span></a><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在系统的设计、开发和实施中</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">借助成熟的开发平台和开发工具</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">吸收相关</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的系统开发中的成功经验</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">力求使系统满足规范要求、易学易用、扩充灵活、安全可靠</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">以提高企业信息管理水平。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(1)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">实用性</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">实用性是该系统设计时要遵循的首要原则。系统的实用性是衡量信息系统的建设成功与否的基本标准</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">是系统为企业创造效益</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">提高企业管理水</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">平的一个重要保证。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(2)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">可靠性</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">该系统中的部分数据设计到公司的机密</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据的安全保密性也是系统设计时必须要考虑的。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(3)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">可维护性</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统要有比较强的后台管理能力</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">便于公司在使用过程中对系统的用户、用户权限、数据库进行有效的管理。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(4)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">易移植性和扩展性</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">随着公司规模的扩大和公司市场化的发展</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">新系统要能方便地移植到计算能力更强大的计算机上</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">并且方便与外部系统的集成。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(5)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">针对性</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">本系统的开发主要就是根据公司的具体需求而开发</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">是经过实地</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的调查了解而设计的</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统主要就是针对公司的现有需求</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">为了解决现在所存在</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的问题。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923315"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.3.2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">功能目标</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">:</span></a><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">润捷</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">管理中存在的问题以及企业发展现状的要求</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在现有条件的支</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">持下可以设计出系统的功能目标。系统功能如表所示</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="border-collapse:collapse; margin-left:8.3pt; width:397.65pt"><tr><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:66.3pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">功能模块</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:309pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">实现功能</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td></tr></table><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="display:none; font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="border-collapse:collapse; margin-left:8.3pt; width:397.65pt"><tr><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:66.3pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">会员管理与供应商管理</span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:309pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">对供应商信息</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">会员</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">信息</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">进行维护管理。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td></tr><tr><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:66.3pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">采购</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">管理</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:309pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">农产品</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">的进货信息</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">和供应商的</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">供货</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">信息的更新和维护</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">管理。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td></tr><tr><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; width:66.3pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">库</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">存</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">管理</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt;
