font-size:10pt">信息</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">以及成品入库信息的维护和管理。</span></p></td></tr><tr><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:66.3pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">商品</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">管理</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:309pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">销售产品</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">的更新和维护管理。</span></p></td></tr><tr><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:66.3pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">订单</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">管理</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:309pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">对进货</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">入库</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">订单</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">等信息进行</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">查询和统计。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td></tr><tr><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:66.3pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 12pt; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">员工</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">管理</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt"> </span></p></td><td style="border-bottom-color:#000000; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-width:0.75pt; border-left-color:#000000; border-left-style:solid; border-left-width:0.75pt; border-right-color:#000000; border-right-style:solid; border-right-width:0.75pt; border-top-color:#000000; border-top-style:solid; border-top-width:0.75pt; padding-left:5.03pt; padding-right:5.03pt; vertical-align:middle; width:309pt"><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-indent:24pt"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image007.png" width="1" height="19" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">对企业的人员</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">信息，</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">工资进行查询和维护管理。</span></p></td></tr></table><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center; text-indent:20pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10pt">表</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10pt">3</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10pt">-2</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923316"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.3.3</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">性能目标</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">:</span></a><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(1)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">准确可靠。要求各种数据准确无误</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">库存反应真实。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(2)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">安全。对于公司的机密信息</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">如客户档案</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">供应商信息</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">进货数据</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">销</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">售数据等</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">只能由相关的人可以获取</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">其他无关人员不能获得。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(3)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">响应速度快</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">界面友好。公司员工在使用中</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">正常情况下</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">应该保证系</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">统运行的速度较快</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">方便用户的输入与浏览。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(4)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">通用性、实用性强</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">操作简单方便。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923317"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">3.4</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">　</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">可能性分析</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对于该公司库管理信息系统的方案也要从经济可行性、技术可行性、使用可</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">行性这三个方面进行分析</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">并论证库存管理信息系统建设的必要性和可能性。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt"> </span><a name="_Toc438923318"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.4.1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">经济可行性</span></a><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">经济可行性的主要任务是对系统进行经济效益的评价</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">评价指标主要分为两部分</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">: </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">费用的支出</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司网络已经相当成熟。从系统硬件要求的配置来讲</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">需要购</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">置一台服务器</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统运行需要的计算机系统</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(Windows XP,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">安装</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">IIS),</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">以及必需配套软件</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">润捷</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">已有安装好的打印机。当然不可量化的维护费用和培训费用也</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在可以接受的范围之内。总体评价费用的花费较少。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">资金的收益</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:(1)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">一次性收益</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">按数据处理、用户、管理和支持等项分类叙述</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">一次性收益有</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">: </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">开支的缩减包括改进了的系统的运行所引起的开支缩减</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">如资源要求的减少</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">, </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">运行效率的改进</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据进入、存贮和恢复技术的改进</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统性能的可监控</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">软件</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的转换和优化</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据压缩技术的采用</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">处理的集中化分布化等</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">; </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">其它如从多余设备出售回收的收入等。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(2)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">非一次性收益</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">该系统能够极大地减少库存采购销售和生产管理等各个方面的费用</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">能减少这一部分工作的人员开支</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">无纸化办公可以节省许多资金。同时</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">计算机软件系</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">统的运行能极大地提高工作效率。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(3)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">不可定量的收益</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">无法直接用人民币表示的收益</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">如服务的改进</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">由操作失误引起的风险的减</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">少</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">信息掌握情况的改进</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">组织机构给外界形象的改善等。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(4)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">潜在收益</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在没有使用系统之前</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">经常会出现库存管理比较混乱而造成产品丢失</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">已经</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">工资管理不精确</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">存在造假现象</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">通过系统的使用可以避免以上情况的发生而减</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">少企业无辜的损失。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923319"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.4.2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">技术可行性</span></a><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统采用</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">my</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">SQL</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据库平台和</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">amuse</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">UI</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">组件</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">进行开发</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">技术优秀的开发平台为整个系统提供了强有力的保证</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">加上优秀的开发人员和完善的开发环境</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">为系统的顺利开发提供了技术保证。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923320"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.4.3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">使用可行性</span></a><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">本信息管理软件是在调查的基础上针对润捷</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">设计开发的</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">用户是具有使用可行性的。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">硬件方面</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司原始已经配置了一定数目的电脑设施和外围设备</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">网络已经全部覆盖</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">需要新添加的设施也已经在计划之列。软件方面</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">该系统开发完成后</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">, </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统界面良好</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">便于操作</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">;</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统移植性能良好</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">;</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">模块与模块之间相互独立</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">库具有保密性。而且在系统开发时</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">完全是根据西裤一厂原有的操作流程和操作习惯开发</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对操作人员进行短期培训就能很快适应系统的运作</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">不必对业务流程</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">进行重大的调整就能运作</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">缩短了开发的时间。另外系统对用户的权限进行了的分层控制</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">使部门中的不同人员既能够使用又不越权。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">因此</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在对新系统开发进行了一系列的可行性分析之后</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">发现新系统已经具备了开发的基础</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">同时也认识到在公司市场化过程中进行管理机制的改造已成为</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">一种必然</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">切合实际的需要。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both" /><p style="font-size:18pt; line-height:150%; margin:5pt 0pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:36.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422763"></a><a name="_Toc438923321"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold"> 第</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">四</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">章</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422763"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">系统需求分析</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">需求分析，是指对要解决的问题进行详细的分析，弄清楚问题的要求，包括需要输入什么数据，要得到什么结果，最后应输出什么。可以说，在软件工程当中的“需求分析”就是确定要计算机“做什么”，要达到什么样的效果。可以说需求分析是做系统之前必做的。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422764"></a><a name="_Toc438923322"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">4</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">.</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">1</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422764"></span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">用例</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><a name="_Toc140422765"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">只有在清楚地了解了企业的需求之后，才能够根据需求而设计出符合企业要求的系统。系统的需求分析是系统开发的重要环节，是系统开发成功的前提。通过对大农合平台业务的分析，对该系统的需求用例模型分析如下：</span></a></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923323"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.1.1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">总经理</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">用例</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image009.png" width="337" height="167" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0.15pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:18.1pt; -aw-wrap-type:topbottom" /><br /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4-1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">总经理</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923324"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.1.2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">公司系统管理员</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image011.png" width="370" height="223" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司系统管理员</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923325"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.1.3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">营运中心负责人</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image013.png" width="272" height="360" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">营运中心</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">负责人</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923326"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.1.4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">员工用例图</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image015.png" width="362" height="288" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 24pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">　</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">员工</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923327"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.1.5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">联络员用例图</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image017.png" width="421" height="265" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">联络员</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923328"><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422765"></span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">4.2</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">　</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">主要</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">功能模块</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">分析</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">由于系统的庞大性与复杂性，现仅分析管理信息系统主要模块及功能的用户需求，需求分析具体如下：</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923329"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.2.1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">商品管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">商品管理模块涉及到类别管理、农户管理和商品信息管理，系统首先添加新类别后，添加能够为大农合平台供应该类别商品的农户信息以及库存信息，最后在添加该类别商品时，通过选择相应的农户及供货顺序，将农户作为移动仓库，和具体商品联系起来，支撑大农合的物流运输管理。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）类别管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">大农合生鲜超市的商品类别添加、修改、删除操作，方便运营人员对商品和农户的管理。同时类别将显示在生鲜超市中，方便用户根据类别筛选和搜索商品。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）农户管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统操作人员可对农户信息和库存信息进行添加、查看、修改、删除操作</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">添加农户：大农合采用以农户为仓库的方式进行库存管理，因此，添加对大农合供货的农户信息，对农户分配联络员，联络员负责联系农户补给库存，方便大农合对农户进行库存管理和物流管理。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">添加库存：添加完农户后，对已签约的农户进行库存的添加，为添加商品时根据库存选择供货的农户做准备，方便订单生成后对相应农户进行物流运输。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）商品管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">大农合可对商品进行添加、编辑、删除、预览、审核和审核结果查询操作，审核通过的商品即可正式上架，在生鲜超市页面显示，供生鲜超市会员购买。同时，可根据商品类别、状态、发售时间、审核时间和商品名称一系列条件进行组合查询商品信息，直观地显示商品的信息，方便运营人员对商品进行管理。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923330"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.2.2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">采购管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">采购管理模块包含的功能有：审核供应商采购、审核供应商供应、发布采购（大农合）、审核采购（大农合）、查看采购竞价、查看已发布采购。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）审核供应商采购</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">供应商在八方集市中提交采购申请后，大农合后台信息系统审核采购信息，审核结果将反映在供应商用户中心，若供应商通过审核，则供应商的采购信息将显示在八方集市中，其他供应商可向该供应商进行供货。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）审核供应商采购</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">供应商在八方集市中提交供应申请后，大农合后台信息系统审核供应信息，审核结果将反映在供应商用户中心，若供应商通过审核，则供应商的供应信息将显示在八方集市中，其他供应商可与该供应商进行供货交易。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）发布采购和审核采购</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">大农合员工可在信息系统填写采购信息，通过上级运营人员审核后，采购信息将在八方集市平台发布，其他供应商可向大农合提出供应申请。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）查看采购竞价</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">大农合发布采购后，可在信息系统中查看采购所对应的竞价信息，查看申请供货的供应商信息及竞价信息，进行信息的审核操作，审核结果将以短信形式通知供应商，并显示在供应商用户中心。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）查看已发布采购</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">该功能用于查看大农合已发布的采购信息，并对八方集市正在显示的采购信息进行关闭操作。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923331"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.2.3 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">会员管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">该模块涉及生鲜超市的会员管理和八方集市的供应商管理。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）会员管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">添加：运营人员可在系统中自行注册生鲜超市账号，方便大农合平台和合作用户的交互。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">查看：通过此操作查看每个会员的具体信息和历史订单。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">查询：通过积分、联系电话和用户名进行组合查询。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）供应商管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">添加：在系统中直接上传供应商资料，注册供应商账号。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">查看：通过此操作查看供应商资料详情。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">审核：八方集市用户自行注册企业账号或注册企业账号后，运营人员在系统中审核供应商信息，审核结果将以短信形式告知供应商并显示在供应商用户中心。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923332"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.2.4 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">权限管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">该模块涉及部门管理、角色管理和员工管理。运营中心负责人通过不同的菜单和按钮对不同的角色进行权限管理，使不同角色的员工在同一系统操作不同的功能。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）部门管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">拥有部门管理权限的员工可在本页面进行部门的添加、删除、修改操作，操作后需要拥有审核权限的上级运营人员进行审核这一系列操作。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）审核部门</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">拥有审核权限的运营人员对部门的操作申请进行审核，若审核通过，则部门的添加、修改、删除等操作真正完成。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）角色管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">拥有该权限的员工可进行员工角色的新增、删除和角色权限的修改操作。在权限操作页面中，用户通过勾选权限来确定左边导航是否出现在角色的操作页面中，以实现权限操作。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）员工管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在员工管理模块可进行员工的添加、修改、删除、查询操作，方便企业人事方面管理。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923333"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">4.3</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">　</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">数据建模</span></a></p><h3 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc140422766"></a><a name="_Toc438923334"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">4.3.1</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422766"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">基本概念</span></a></h3><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据模型通常由数据结构、数据操作和完整性约束三部分组成，是严格定义的一组概念的集合，精确的描述了系统的静态特写、动态特性和完整性约束条件。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">概念模型用于信息世界的建模，是现实世界到信息世界的第一层抽象，是数据库设计人员进行数据库设计的有力的工具，也是设计人员与用户之间进行交流的语言。信息世界涉及的概念主要有：</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1.</span><span style="width:3pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">实体（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Entity</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）：客观存在并可相互区别的事物成为实体。可以是人、事、物，也可以是抽象的概念和联系。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2.</span><span style="width:3pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">属性（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Attribute</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）：实体所具有的某一特性。一个实体可以又若干个属性来刻画。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3.</span><span style="width:3pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">码（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Key</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）：唯一标识实体的属性集。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4.</span><span style="width:3pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">域（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Domain</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）：域是一组具有相同数据类型的值的集合。属性的取值范围来自某个域。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5.</span><span style="width:3pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">实体型（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Entity Type</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）：具有相同属性的实体必然具有共同的特征和性质。用实体名和属性名集合来抽象和刻画同类实体，称为实体型。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6.</span><span style="width:3pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">实体集（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Entity Set</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">:</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">同一类型实体的集合。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">7.</span><span style="width:3pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">联系（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Relationship</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）：实体内部和实体之间的联系。实体之间的联系有一对一，一对多、多对多三种。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc140422767"></a><a name="_Toc438923335"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">新建概念数据模型</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422767"></span></a></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">部门，员工，权限，按钮，菜单；</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">农户，库存，商品；</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">用户，供应商，订单；</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">采购供应，竞价；</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">类别；</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><h3 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc140422769"></a><a name="_Toc438923336"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">4.3.3</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422769"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">添加实体</span></a></h3><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">第一大模块</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">部门表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image019.png" width="436" height="82" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">-6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">部门表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">员工表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image021.png" width="408" height="222" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">-7</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">员工表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">角色表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image023.png" width="403" height="58" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">-8</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">角色表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">按钮表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image025.png" width="440" height="103" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">-9</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">按钮</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">菜单表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image027.png" width="420" height="106" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">-10</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">菜单表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">权限表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image029.png" width="369" height="107" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">-11</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">权限表</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">第二大模块</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify;
