font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="color:#333333; font-family:Arial; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="color:#333333; font-family:Arial; font-size:10.5pt">-23</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">员工，部门，角色之间的联系</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">一个部门有多个员工，一个角色有多个员工，权限的分配市对应角色来说的，当此员工对应该角色时，就具有该角色的权限。权限分为菜单权限和按钮权限。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="color:#333333; font-family:Arial; font-size:10.5pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image053.png" width="355" height="341" alt="C:\Users\zhang\Desktop\qw.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="color:#333333; font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="color:#333333; font-family:Arial; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="color:#333333; font-family:Arial; font-size:10.5pt">-24</span><span style="color:#333333; font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">农户，农户库存，和商品之间的联系</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="color:#333333; font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">一个农户有多个产品库存，多个产品库存组成商品库存。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image055.png" width="340" height="776" alt="C:\Users\zhang\Desktop\aa.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="color:#333333; font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="color:#333333; font-family:Arial; font-size:10.5pt">4</span><span style="color:#333333; font-family:Arial; font-size:10.5pt">-25</span><span style="color:#333333; font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">用户，供应商，订单，订单详情之间的联系</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="color:#333333; font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">用户，供应商下定单，一个订单可以有多个订单详情。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="color:#333333; font-family:Arial; font-size:10.5pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image057.png" width="500" height="664" alt="C:\Users\zhang\Desktop\qwqwqw.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-26</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">竞价信息和供应商之间的联系</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">每一个供应商都可以发采购和供应，对应别的供应商可以竞价，同时，供应商也可以对大农合的采购信息进行竞价。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image059.png" width="250" height="204" alt="C:\Users\zhang\Desktop\assa.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-27</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">类别自连接形成树</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">类别自连接</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">fanumber</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对应</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">number</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">产生一个树，从而产生对类别的管理。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923338"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">4.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">3.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">5 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">检查概念数据模型完整性</span></a></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">关系数据库的完整性：实体完整型、参照完整性、用户自定义完整性，其中实体完整性和参照完整性是关系模型必须满足的完整性约束条件，被称作关系的两个不变特性。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">实体完整性规则：若</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">A</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">是关系</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">R</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的主属性，则</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">A</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">不能取控制，即主属性不能为空。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">参照完整性规则：如</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">F</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">是关系</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">R</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的外码，参照关系</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的主码</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">K</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">，则</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">R</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">中每个元祖在</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">F</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">上的值必须为</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">中某个元祖的主码值或空值，即外码要么是参照的主码值要么是空值。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">用户自定义完整性：对身份证，手机号的唯一标识。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both" /><h1 style="font-size:18pt; line-height:150%; margin:5pt 0pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:36.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923339"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold"> 第</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">五</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">章</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">系统设计</span></a></h1><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统设计是新系统的物理设计阶段。根据系统分析阶段所确定的新系统的逻辑模型、功能要求，在用户提供的环境条件下，设计出一个能在计算机网络环境上实施的方案，即建立新系统的物理模型。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923340"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">5</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">1</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold"> </span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统的体系结构设计</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">随着信息系统规模不断扩大、复杂程度日益提高，体系结构模式对信息系统性能的影响越来越大不同功能的信息系统对体系结构模式有不同的要求，各种体系结构模式的信息系统在开发和应用过程中也有很大的区别。选择和设计合理的体系结构模式甚至比算法设计和数据结构设计更重要。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">随着</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Internet/Intranet </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的普及</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">传统的客户</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">/</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">服务器</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(Client/Server C/S)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">也渐渐被基于网络为基础的三层浏览器</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">/</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">服务器</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(Browser/Server B/S)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所替代。</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">结构如下图：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image061.jpg" width="569" height="101" alt="C:\Users\Administrator\Desktop\BS结构图.jpg" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">从本质上看，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">结构也是一种</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">C/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">结构，在这种结构下，用户工作界面通过浏览器来实现，极少部分事务逻辑在前端（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Browser</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）实现，主要事务逻辑在服务器端（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Server</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）实现，形成所谓三层结构。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">结构主要利用了不断成熟的</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Web</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">浏览器技术：结合浏览器的多种脚本语言和</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">ActiveX</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">技术，用通用浏览器实现原来需要复杂专用软件才能实现的强大功能，同时节约了开发成本。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">结构的使用越来越多，特别是由需求推动了</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">AJAX</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">技术的发展，它的程序也能在客户端电脑上进行部分处理，从而大大的减轻了服务器的负担；并增加了交互性，能进行局部实时刷新。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">结构的优点可以归纳成以下三点：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">维护和升级方式简单。当前，软件系统的改进和升级越发频繁，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">架构的产品明显体现着更为方便的特性。对一个稍微大一点单位来说，系统管理人员如果需要在几百甚至上千部电脑之间来回奔跑，效率和工作量是可想而知的，但</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">架构的软件只需要管理服务器就行了，所有的客户端只是浏览器，根本不需要做任何的维护。无论用户的规模有多大，有多少分支机构都不会增加任何维护升级的工作量，所有的操作只需要针对服务器进行；如果是异地，只需要把服务器连接专网即可，实现远程维护、升级和共享。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">成本降低，选择更多。大家都知道</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">windows</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在桌面电脑上几乎一统天下，浏览器成为了标准配置，但在服务器操作系统上</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">windows</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">并不是处于绝对的统治地位。 当前的趋势是凡使用</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">架构的应用管理软件，只需安装在</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Linux</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">服务器上即可，而且安全性高。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">应用服务器运行数据负荷较重。由于</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">架构管理软件只安装在服务器端（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Server</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）上，网络管理人员只需要管理服务器就行了，用户界面主要事务逻辑在服务器（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Server</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）端完全通过</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">WWW</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">浏览器实现，极少部分事务逻辑在前端（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Browser</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）实现，所有的客户端只有浏览器，网络管理人员只需要做硬件维护。但是，应用服务器运行数据负荷较重，一旦发生服务器“崩溃”等问题，后果不堪设想。因此，许多单位都备有数据库存储服务器，以防万一。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">根据实际所需与润大农合公司的意见，我们开发的系统结构选择</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">结构。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923341"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">5</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">.</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">2</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统页面布局设计</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统的页面设计主要是以简洁，清晰的风格，给客户带来使用简单，信息一目了然的体验。同时根据</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">B/S</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">结构的使用原则，我们系统在设计时也考虑了以下几点：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">页面最小：由于</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Web</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的网络特性，尽可能减小单页面加载量，降低图片文件大小和数量，加快加载速度，方便用户体验。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">屏幕适应：</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Web</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">界面需要适应不同用户屏幕大小。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">浏览器兼容：需要适应不同浏览器浏览效果，虽然目前可不考虑不同浏览器差别，但仍需考虑</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">IE</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">浏览器版本差异带来的客户端不同效果。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">最少垂直滚动：尽可能减少垂直方向滚动，尽可能不超过两屏。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">禁止水平滚动：由于将导致非常恶劣的客户体验，尽可能禁止浏览器水平滚动操作。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">避免隐藏（右键）操作：浏览器的右键操作不符合用户体验习惯，尽可能避免</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">一</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">)</span><span style="width:30.67pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">页面整体风格</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统的各个页面都将采取与以下相似的布局以及色彩的搭配：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image063.png" width="494" height="261" alt="C:\Users\Administrator\Desktop\系统风格.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">页面</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">布局</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">页面主要分为三部分，上部为标题横幅，下部左半部分为菜单、导航栏，而占据较大部分的下部右半部分为各个页面的主要内容。而页面的色调主要以白色、浅灰色等较浅色系为主，使页面看起来简洁而不单调，层次分明，让使用者有较好的观感体验。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">二</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">)</span><span style="width:30.67pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">CSS </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Javascript</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">和</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Ajax</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">的使用</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在保持系统各模块页面的样式一致上，我们将每个页面统一的部分，例如图片，文字格式，颜色等样式放在</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">CSS</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">里，然后每个页面在设计时只要引用这个</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">CSS</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">文件即可做到页面风格统一的效果。而在某些页面里的特效，我们使用了</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">js</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">脚本实现，并且使用了</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Ajax</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">技术，让页面可以不刷新也能做到前后台数据的交互，大大改善了用户的使用体验。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923342"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">5.</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">3</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统功能设计</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统功能设计常常使用 </span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">HIPO </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">技术来进行系统设计、评价，在系统实施之前加工和修改已设计的系统。此技术不仅可以使用户、管理人员和其他系统建设者很方便地理解系统的程序结构，也便于程序的编写和修改。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">HIPO</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Hierarchy plus Input/Process/Output</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）技术：用图形的方法表达一个系统的输入输出功能以及模块层次。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">HIPO</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">分层图：表示自顶向下分解所有的模块层次结构。本系统的</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">HIPO</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">分层：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image065.png" width="554" height="422" alt="C:\Users\Administrator\Desktop\HIPO.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">功能设计</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923343"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">5.4</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">数据库设计</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据库设计是指对于一个给定的应用环境，构造优化得数据库逻辑模式和物理结构，并据此建立数据库及其应用系统，使之能够有效地存储和管理数据，满足各种用户的应用需求</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">包括信息管理要求和数据操作要求。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据库设计中，我们采用的是实体</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">关系图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(E-R</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">来进行概念模型设计，如下：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image067.png" width="505" height="806" alt="C:\Users\Administrator\Desktop\E-R.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">数据</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">库</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923344"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">5.</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">5</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统安全性设计</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">权限控制机制</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">权限控制指的是在一开始角色创立时已分配了不同权限，然后在不同用户登录时将通过权限判断，从而显示不同的菜单、导航栏，限制了其活动，从而做到区分开不同角色的访问，保证了公司机密的安全。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">以下分别是管理员与联络员登录后的导航栏：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image069.png" width="190" height="285" alt="C:\Users\Administrator\Desktop\联络员.png" style="-aw-left-pos:208.85pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0.75pt; -aw-wrap-type:square; float:left; margin:0pt 9pt" /><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image071.png" width="235" height="664" alt="C:\Users\Administrator\Desktop\管理员.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0.45pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0.75pt; -aw-wrap-type:tight; float:left; margin:0pt 9pt" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">权限</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">用户身份验证</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">用户安全登陆问题本质上是用户身份验证的问题。身份验证是指用户向系统</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">出示自己的身份证明过程。身份认证是系统查核用户的身份证明的过程。人们常</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">把这两项工作统称为身份验证</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">(</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">或身份鉴别</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">)</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">，是判明和确认通信双方真实身份的</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">两个重要环节。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">润大农合信息管理系统的用户安全登录我们使用的是用户名和密码进行验证。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">如图：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image073.png" width="488" height="48" alt="C:\Users\Administrator\Desktop\登录.png" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /><span style="width:388.3pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block; -aw-tabstop-align:right; -aw-tabstop-pos:415.3pt"></span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">登录</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）</span><span style="width:18pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">物理安全</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">本系统的使用对象主要是润大农合的员工，属于企业内部网，系统中存放着企业的重要的商业机密，所以最好的安全措施就是实施物理隔绝，建立企业内部局域网，在物理上与 </span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Internet </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">网络隔绝。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对于服务器的管理与维护，要经常对数据库进行备份操作，防止数据的丢失</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">和损坏。</span><span style="width:36pt; text-indent:0pt; display:inline-block"></span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923345"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">5.6 </span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">物理配置方案</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、计算机系统的硬件配置</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">计算机系统的硬件配置方案的设计应考虑以下因素：系统吞吐量、系统响应时间、系统可靠性、数据管理的方式、地域范围等。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">根据系统调查和系统分析的结果来考虑系统的物理结构和硬件配置，并结合本公司的实际情况和所选用的软件开发工具及数据库系统的特点来综合进行物理配置方案的设计。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">目前，公司以配置内部局域网络，因此系统可在公司局域网上直接运行。网络服务器上安装后台数据库和执行共享资源的管理应用程序，其余计算机可以通过浏览器直接访问本系统，所以系统维护也比较方便。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、开发工具</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">软件开发环境：</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Java8</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Java EE Eclipse</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Tomcat8.0</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">MySQL Server 5.6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">。</span></p><p style="font-size:18pt; line-height:150%; margin:5pt 0pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:36.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422770"><br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both" /></a><a name="_Toc438923346"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">第</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">章</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422770"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">系统实现</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">和</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">系统维护</span></a></p><h2 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422771"></a><a name="_Toc438923347"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">1</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">  </span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold"> </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422771"></span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统使用流程图</span></a></h2><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">管理信息系统处理方式的合理选择，是一个处理过程的设计问题。选择处理方式实际上就是根据系统的任务、目标和环境条件，合理选择信息活动的形式及其具体方法。程序流程图又称程序框图，表示方法简明扼要。为了简单直观的描述本系统的处理过程，采用活动流程图来描述程序执行的逻辑过程。它把程序的基本步骤归纳为输入、输出、处理及结束等几个过程。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">本系统主要是在用户登录系统之后，根据用户的权限进入系统各个功能版块进行操作。</span></p><h3 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc140422772"></a><a name="_Toc438923348"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">.1.1  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422772"></span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">设计</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:normal">方法</span></a></h3><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">采用自顶向下的模块设计方法</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">，</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">将系统程序流程图展示如下图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image075.png" width="610" height="394" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">流程</span></p><h2 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:173%; margin:13pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422773"></a><a name="_Toc438923349"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">6.2.</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422773"></span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统界面实现</span></a></h2><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923350"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">首页</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">展示生鲜超市的数据有：用户数量、实时在线用户、用户成交订单、用户积分总量；展示后台系统的数据有：商品销量图表、在线员工统计、员工任务等。通过展示简单直观的数据，使后台操作人员更加了解生鲜超市页面的运营状况。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image077.png" width="591" height="353" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-2 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">后台首页</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923351"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">部门管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">部门管理：拥有部门管理权限的员工可在本页面进行部门的添加、删除、修改操作，操作后需要拥有审核权限的上级运营人员进行审核这一系列操作。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image079.png" width="555" height="235" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-3 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">部门列表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">审核部门：拥有审核权限的运营人员对部门的操作申请进行审核，若审核通过，则部门的添加、修改、删除等操作真正完成。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image081.png" width="554" height="258" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">6-4 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">审核部门</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21.1pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt; font-weight:bold">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923352"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">角色管理</span></a></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">拥有该权限的员工可进行员工角色的新增、删除和角色权限的修改操作。在权限操作页面中，用户通过勾选权限来确定左边导航是否出现在角色的操作页面中，以实现权限操作。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">6-5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">和图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">6-6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">所示：</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image083.png" width="361" height="273" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">-5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">权限</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">管理</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image085.png" width="501" height="530" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">权限管理</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923353"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">员工管理</span></a></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">在员工管理模块可进行员工的添加、修改、删除、查询操作，方便企业对员工的人事方面管理。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">6-7</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">和图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">6-8</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">所示：</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image087.png" width="543" height="314" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt;
