font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-7</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">员工列表</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image089.png" width="550" height="339" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">6-</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">8</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">员工</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">添加</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923354"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">会员管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">会员管理模块用于对生鲜超市会员的添加、查询、查看详情、修改、查看历史订单等操作，方便后台人员查看前台页面用户信息，便于会员管理。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-9</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">和图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-10</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image091.png" width="555" height="291" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-9 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">会员管理</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image093.png" width="554" height="215" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-10 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">查看历史订单</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923355"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">供应商管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">    供应商列表：添加、查看供应商详细信息，方便运营人员进行供应商管理。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-11</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image095.png" width="491" height="606" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-11</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">供应商添加</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">审核供应商：八方集市的企业注册、个人升级企业申请提交后，在该页面进行供应商信息的审核，审核结果将以短信形式发送给供应商，同时在八方及时用户中心体现，方便供应商用户及时得知审核结果，并对审核信息进行查看。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-12</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image097.png" width="554" height="228" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-12</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">审核供应商</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923356"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.7</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">类别管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">    此页面用于大农合生鲜超市的商品类别添加、修改、删除操作，以方便运营人员对商品和农户的管理。同时类别将显示在生鲜超市中，方便用户根据类别筛选和搜索商品。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-13</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image099.png" width="354" height="477" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-13</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">类别</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">管理</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923357"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.8</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">农户管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">    添加农户：大农合采用以农户为仓库的方式进行库存管理，因此，此页面用于添加对大农合供货的农户信息，对农户分配联络员，联络员负责联系农户补给库存，方便大农合对农户进行库存管理和物流管理。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-14</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">和图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-15</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image101.png" width="554" height="316" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-14</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">农户</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">添加</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">添加库存：添加完农户后，对已签约的农户进行库存的添加，用于添加商品时根据库存选择供货的农户，方便订单生成后对相应农户进行物流运输。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-15</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image103.png" width="554" height="275" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">15</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">添加</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">库存</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923358"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.9</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">商品管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">    可根据商品类别、状态、发售时间、审核时间和商品名称一系列条件进行组合查询商品信息；可对商品进行添加、编辑、删除、预览、审核和审核结果查询操作，直观地显示商品的信息，方便运营人员对商品进行管理。如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-16</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-17</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">和图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-18</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image105.png" width="568" height="614" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-16</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">商品</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">列表</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image107.png" width="487" height="549" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-17</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">商品</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">添加</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image109.png" width="556" height="131" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-18</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">审核</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">商品</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923359"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.2.10</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">采购管理</span></a></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">    八方集市中供应商提交采购申请后，大农合后台信息系统审核采购信息，审核结果将反映在供应商用户中心，方便供应商查看自己的采购审核结果，如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-19</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示。大农合在后台发布采购信息后，八方集市的供应商可申请向大农合竞价供货，供货信息可在“查看采购竞价”页面查看并审核，审核结果将以短信形式发送给相应的供应商，同时显示在该供应商用户中心，如图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6-20</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image111.png" width="512" height="206" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-19</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">审核</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">供应商</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><img src="http://zhangpengpengfei.github.io/wangzhan/images-folder/image101.png" width="560" height="256" alt="" style="-aw-left-pos:0pt; -aw-rel-hpos:column; -aw-rel-vpos:paragraph; -aw-top-pos:0pt; -aw-wrap-type:inline" /></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:center; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-20</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">查看</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">采购竞价</span></p><h2 style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422774"></a><a name="_Toc438923360"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">3</span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold"> </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422774"></span><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold"> </span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">代码实现</span></a></h2><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">后台管理信息系统采用工厂方法模式，对简单工厂模式进行了抽象。有一个抽象的</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Factory</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">类（可以是抽象类和接口），这个类将不在负责具体的产品生产，而是只制定一些规范，具体的生产工作由其子类去完成。在这个模式中，工厂类和产品类往往可以依次对应。即一个抽象工厂对应一个抽象产品，一个具体工厂对应一个具体产品，这个具体的工厂就负责生产对应的产品。　</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32.15pt"><a name="_Toc438923361"><span style="font-family:Arial; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">6.4</span><span style="font-family:黑体; font-size:16pt; font-weight:bold">系统测试与维护</span></a></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统测试是系统开发周期中一个十分重要而漫长的阶段。其重要性体现在它是保证系统质量与可靠性的最后关口，是对整个系统开发过程包括系统分析，系统设计和系统实现的最终审查。系统测试的对象不仅仅是源程序，而应是整个系统，它把需求分析，概要设计，详细设计以及程序设计各阶段的开发文档，包括需求规格说明，概要设计说明，详细设计说明以及源程序，都作为测试的对象。测试的目的就是发现系统的错误。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc140422775"></a><a name="_Toc438923362"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.4</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">.1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">系统测试的原则</span></a><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">  </span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422775"></span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）测试工作应避免由原开发系统的个人或小组来承担。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）设计测试方案时，不仅要包括确定的输入数据，而且包括从系统功能出发预期的测试结果。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）测试用例不仅要包括合理，有效的输入数据，还要包括无效的或不合理的输入数据。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）不仅要检验程序是否做了该做的事，还要检查程序是否同时做了不该做的事。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）保留测试用例，作为软件文档的组成部分。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923363"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.4.2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">系统测试的方法</span></a></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统测试一般有单元测试，组装测试，确认测试和系统测试四个步骤，每一步都是在前一步的基础上进行的。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）单元测试</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">单元测试是测试程序模块及其接口与设计说明的要求是否一致，目的是发现程序编写阶段的错误。它以单个程序模块为测试单位。单元测试采用白盒测试的方法，根据详细设计的描述，从模块的内部结构出发设计测试用例，进行测试。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">由于每个模块在整个软件中不是孤立的，尽管它可以单独编译，但不能单独进行测试。因此在测试时，应考虑它与调用和被调用模块的相互联系。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）组装测试</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对每个模块完成了单元测试以后，需要按照设计时做出的层次模块图把它们连接起来，进行组装测试。在资料管理信息系统中我采用了自底向上测试的组装顺序。先从一个底层模块开始，从下向上逐步添加模块，组成和程序的一个分支，对每个分支重复上述过程，直到所有的分支组装完成。最后将所有分支组成整个程序。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）确认测试</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">功能测试：检测系统需求规格说明书的内容是否全部实现。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">性能测试：检查系统的可移植性，兼容性，错误恢复能力以及可维护性等性能指标，以检测系统功能实现的程序。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">配置审查：检查被测系统的全部构成是否齐全，质量是否合乎要求，应有维护所需的全部细节，并且是否编好目录。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）系统测试</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统测试是将信息系统的所有组成部分包括软件，硬件，用户以及环境等综合在一起进行测试，要在系统的实际运行环境现场，在用户的直接参与下进行。包括集成功能测试，可靠性与适应性测试，系统自我保护及恢复能力的测试，安全性测试，强度测试。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923364"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.4.3 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">系统运行与维护</span></a></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">网站在完成系统实施，投入正常运行之后，就进入了系统运行与维护阶段。在系统的整个使用寿命中，都将伴随着系统维护工作的进行。系统维护的目的是保证管理信息</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">系统正常而可靠地运行，并能使系统不断得到改善和提高，以充分发挥作用，系统维护的内容可分为以下几类： </span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）程序的维护：在系统投入运行之后，程序中的问题不断体现出来，而且用户对系统随时提出新的要求，所以要及时对系统作些修改或扩展系统功能，从而改正错误和满足用户的新要求。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）数据的维护：数据的维护主要是指对数据文件内容的增加、删除、修改以及数据的备份等。备份由计算机完成或人工在操作系统下完成。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）机器的维护：计算机及其外部设备在使用中会发生故障，所以要对计算机进行及时的维修，更换损坏部件，加强管理，以保证系统正常运行。</span></p><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:150%; margin:13pt 0pt 5pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:32pt"><a name="_Toc438923365"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:16pt">6.4.4 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt">系统评价</span></a></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">本系统从面向使用的角度，利用</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">JSP+Servlet</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">技术的管理系统基本实现了对系统的基本功能，它具有以下特点：</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）较全面地录入、维护、查询、统计功能，可以取代手工操作，有较强的数据处理能力。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）友好的用户界面。通过用鼠标操作准确方便，界面清晰，便于用户在短时间内熟悉，掌握操作方法。</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">（</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">）程序易懂易维护。程序的编写做到了结构化、模块化，结构整齐清晰，条例明确，易读易维护。</span></p><h1 style="font-size:18pt; line-height:150%; margin:5pt 0pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:36.15pt"><a name="_Toc140422777"><br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both" /></a><a name="_Toc438923366"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">7</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">　</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">第七章</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">结束语</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422777"></span></a></h1><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在为润捷公司搭建农产品电子商务平台期间</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">经过调研</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对公司运营流程已经比较熟悉。 </span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">我对公司的管理流程及存在的问题进行了广泛深入的调研</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">对企业的生产、 管理、信息化建设等方面有了更加深入的了解。尤其是针对公司的客户资源管理 和服务方面存在的问题和经理进行了深入的分析和探讨</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">了解了问题产生的根本原因</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">提出了解决问题的一些方法。在此期间</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">我将在书本上学到的理论知识应用到实践中</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">一方面能够更好的发现公司所存在的问题</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">另一方面</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">也加深 了我对理论知识的理解。 </span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">公司运营等方面的知识已经比较熟悉。同时我还不断的项目经理沟通交流</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">了解有公司目前所存在的问题</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">以及系统需要实现哪些方面的功能。在了解中</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">我们发现公司所存在的问题在于两大方面</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">, </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">一是库存管理</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">由于公司都是按照订单生产</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所以经常存在一些尾单留在仓库 之中</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">这个单纯的依靠人工来统计</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">不但准确性不高</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">而且容易造成库存的丢失 等等方面的问题。另一个是公司的人员管理问题</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">经常会信息有误带来损失。 </span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">通过以上对公司实地调查和分析</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">根据企业的实际需求</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">我设计了此系统</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">本系统在功能方面比较完善</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">操作也简便</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">易于员工接受。更为重要的是 加快了企业信息的传递速度</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">共享企业的基本信息</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">使得润捷的管理更上一个台阶</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">,</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">为在激烈的市场竞争中增强了竞争力。</span><span style="color:#ff0000; font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt"> </span></p><br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both" /><h1 style="font-size:18pt; line-height:150%; margin:5pt 0pt 0pt; page-break-after:avoid; page-break-inside:avoid; text-align:justify; text-indent:24.1pt"><a name="_Toc140422779"></a><a name="_Toc438923367"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:18pt; font-weight:bold">主要参考文献</span><span style="-aw-bookmark-end:_Toc140422779"></span></a></h1><p style="font-size:10.5pt; font-size:10.5pt"> </span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">[2] </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">《</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">图论</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">》</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; font-size:10.5pt; text-decoration:underline">http://www.w3school.com.cn/</span></a><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">  jQuery</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">选择器</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; font-size:10.5pt">   java </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">分页视频</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">[</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">5</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">]</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt"> </span><a href="http://study.163.com/course/courseMain.htm?courseId=943007"><span style="color:#0000ff; font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt; text-decoration:underline">http://study.163.com/course/courseMain.htm?courseId=943007</span></a><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">  java</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">核心技术</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">[</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">6</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">]</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt"> </span><a href="http://deerchao.net/tutorials/regex/regex.htm"><span style="color:#0000ff; font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt; text-decoration:underline">http://deerchao.net/tutorials/regex/regex.htm</span></a><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">正则表达式</span></p><p style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">[</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">7</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">]</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt"> </span><a href="https://saas.hpe.com/zh-cn/download/loadrunner"><span style="color:#0000ff; font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt; text-decoration:underline">https://saas.hpe.com/zh-cn/download/loadrunner</span></a><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">  </span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:10.5pt">loadrunner</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">压力测试</span></p><br style="page-break-before:always; clear:both" /><p style="font-size:16pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:21pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:16pt; font-style:italic; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">关于课程设计的说明：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、封面必须完全统一，只需要将“</span><span style="color:#993300; font-family:楷体_GB2312; font-size:18pt">××管理信息系统</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">”</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">改成自己所选择的题目。小组名单每行只写三到四人，人数超出分两行写。邮箱写一个联系人的即可。时间写成课程设计进行的月份，不需要到日期。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">封面采用浅绿色封皮进行装订。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、第</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">页</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">前半部分</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">不需要做改动，只需要在第二张表中增加本小组学生的班级、学号、姓名即可。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、第</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">页开始为目录，</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">目录在设计完成后直接点右键，选择更新域即可，注意</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">在下一步弹出选择框时要选</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">更新整个目录。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、选题说明主要对自己选该题目的原因、意义，以及该题目的特点等进行简单的描述。基本思路主要是本小组对该题目确定后如何着手工作，逻辑顺序情况如何进行分析。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt; font-style:italic; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">小组分工情况必须要写明，这是大家最终得分一个重要参考项目。最后请务必不要忘记对自己的工作进行一个自我评定。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">这个自我评定统一 在打印装订后手工打勾。在答辩时会针对自我评定的不同情况进行难度不同的问题要求，因此务请实事求是。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">各章节标题号后没有任何标点，只空一格。标题后也没有任何标点，标题为名词或名词短语形式，不允许出现动词、形容词以及语气。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">6</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">页眉中“</span><span style="color:#ff6600; font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt; font-weight:bold">《管理信息系统》课程设计——《××管理信息系统》</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">”应该根据所选题目更改。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">7</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、摘要主要内容是自己的工作，不要对理论和背景、意义等大篇幅进行介绍。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">字数在</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">300-400</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">字左右，关键词</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">3-5</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">个。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">8</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、结束语主要是自己对自己编写的系统、报告的评价，以及对自己工作的总结、收获等内容。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">9</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、致谢部分可有可无，但是如果有</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">务必</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">要实事求是。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">10</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、参考文献的格式如下所述：</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">[</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">]</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">金江军、潘懋．现代物流</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">[M]</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">．北京：北京大学出版社，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2003</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">[2]</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">周耿、涂志玲、彭磊．逆向物流浅析</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">[J]</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">．管理现代化，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2003.2</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">[3]</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">石付恒．煤炭物流系统的研究</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">[D]</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">．</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">[</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">中国矿业大学硕士学位论文</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">]</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">．中国矿业大学图书馆，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2004</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">[4]</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">陈柳钦</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:10.5pt">．</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">有关环保物流的理论探讨</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">. www.56net.</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">com</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">2005.10</span></p><p style="font-size:12pt; line-height:130%; margin:0pt; orphans:0; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt; widows:0"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">         </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">上面分别是书籍、刊物、学位论文以及网络资料的格式。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">11</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、课程设计报告格式上原则要求字体为小四，宋体，如果是英文字母或数字要求是 </span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">Times New Roman</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">体。行间距为最小值，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">18</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">磅</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">章节之间请分页。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">12</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、关于出现的图表要进行编号</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图统一编写格式如“图</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1-1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">组织结构图”所示。其中，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1-1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">表示为第一章中的第一个图，后面的是该图的名称。这几个字为隶书，五号字，在图的下方，居中显示。表则统一编写格式如“表</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1-</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1 </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">新旧系统要求对照表</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">”</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">所示。其中，</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1-1</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">表示第一章中的第一个表，后面是该表的名称。这几个字为隶书，五号字，在表的上方，居中显示。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">图表不要跨页。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">13</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、在答辩时顺序随机排定，每组选出一个代表先对小组的主要工作进行一个简要的介绍，限制在</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">10</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">分钟以内。然后进行程序演示，最后是提问。在整个答辩期间，小组的所有成员均可参加，在回答问题时可以一起回答，不限定于某个具体的同学。在某一组答辩时，其它组的成员不得在场。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">4</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、最后所交的内容为两部分：一是打印的报告，一是电子版的报告和可运行的程序（注意：要生成可执行文件）。如果有</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">PPT</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">讲稿也交。将所有的这些资料压缩在一个文件夹下，</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">上传到作业邮箱</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">。</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">如果本小组的答辩顺序编号为</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">12</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">组，则文件名称为：</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">12</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">组</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">-</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">某某管理信息系统。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">15</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">、为了减少打印、装订</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">成本，答辩时的打印稿可以不装订。打印之前可以先把电子稿给老师</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">看一下。在所有小组答辩结束后</span><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">1~2</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">天内交上修改后的打印装订稿，装订完成后一定要记住小组自评成绩务必要打上。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:'Times New Roman'; font-size:12pt">&#xa0;</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt; font-weight:normal">       </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt; font-weight:normal; text-decoration:underline"> </span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:14pt; font-weight:bold; text-decoration:underline">报告的格式规范性非常重要，任何工作必须都要规范，否则无法保证质量，这一点请大家务必重视。在答辩时请带上自己的报告打印稿。</span></p><p style="line-height:18pt; margin:0pt; text-align:justify; text-indent:24pt"><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">        希望</span><span style="font-family:宋体; font-size:12pt">大家通过课程设计能有所收获！</span></p></div></body></html>
